| **Concern** | **S40 primary mandate** = TD-S37-01 closure (P1 carry-forward from S39 — hardcoded `0.3::numeric AS tau_pin` + `0.3::numeric AS tau_accel` in ENH-81 SQL views to formalize as `merdian_parameters` runtime lookup via `get_parameter_num('pin.tau.'||symbol)::numeric AS tau_used` per ADR-016 parameter calibration pattern) + opportunistic Marketview v4 atomic-card redesign per operator critique of single-Hero rollup layout violating ADR-017 P1 three-filter rule. **TD-S37-01 closure path:** `patch_s40_enh83_view_tau_rewrite.py` v3-pattern (BOM-safe `read_bytes() + decode('utf-8-sig')` + predominant-EOL preservation via `write_bytes(text.encode(enc))` preventing Windows CRLF corruption + `ast.parse` validation before file write + `_PRE_S40.sql` backups per file + idempotency guards + cp1252 fix from initial draft surfacing as TD-S40-NEW-1 S4 cosmetic-only no-behavior-change in the patch script itself); operator ran dry-run → live → reapplied both view DDLs (`sql/2026-05-25_enh81_v_gex_strike_pin_zone.sql` + `sql/2026-05-25_enh81_v_gex_strike_accel_zone.sql`) via Supabase SQL editor → smoke-fire `SELECT DISTINCT tau_used FROM v_gex_strike_pin_zone WHERE symbol IN ('NIFTY','SENSEX')` returned 0.30 cross-symbol = ENH-83 runtime lookup against `merdian_parameters` working end-to-end. **TD-S40-NEW-2 emergent same-session:** post-patch attempted `update_parameter('pin.tau.NIFTY', 'S40 smoke-test', p_value_num := 0.25)` round-trip → `ERROR: new row for relation "merdian_parameters" violates check constraint "chk_valid_from_to"`. SQL forensics on `information_schema.columns` revealed `valid_to` had `column_default = now()`; PL/pgSQL function execution = one transaction, so `now()` returns transaction-timestamp identical for `valid_from` and `valid_to` → CHECK `(valid_from < valid_to OR valid_to IS NULL)` rejected. Fix `ALTER TABLE public.merdian_parameters ALTER COLUMN valid_to DROP DEFAULT;` zero-downtime; verified 0.30→0.25→0.30 round-trip produced clean temporal chain (old row valid_to=now_T1, new row valid_from=now_T1 NULL valid_to). ### Phase 1 — TD-S37-01 closure

`patch_s40_enh83_view_tau_rewrite.py` v3-pattern: BOM-safe `read_bytes() + decode('utf-8-sig')`; predominant-EOL preservation `write_bytes(text.encode(enc))` (prevents Windows CRLF corruption); `ast.parse` validation before file write; `_PRE_S40.sql` backups per file; idempotency guard via grep for `get_parameter_num`; cp1252 fix from initial draft surfaced as TD-S40-NEW-1 S4 cosmetic-only. Operator ran dry-run → live → reapplied both ENH-81 view DDLs via Supabase SQL editor → smoke-fire `SELECT DISTINCT tau_used FROM v_gex_strike_pin_zone WHERE symbol IN ('NIFTY','SENSEX')` returned 0.30 for both = ENH-83 runtime lookup against `merdian_parameters` working end-to-end.

### Phase 2 — TD-S40-NEW-2 DISCOVERED + FIXED same-session

Post-patch flexed `update_parameter('pin.tau.NIFTY', 'S40 smoke-test', p_value_num := 0.25)` → `ERROR: new row for relation "merdian_parameters" violates check constraint "chk_valid_from_to"`. SQL forensics on `information_schema.columns` showed `valid_to` column had `column_default = now()`; PL/pgSQL function execution = one transaction, so `now()` returns transaction-timestamp identical for `valid_from` and `valid_to`. Fix: `ALTER TABLE public.merdian_parameters ALTER COLUMN valid_to DROP DEFAULT;`. Verified 0.30→0.25→0.30 round-trip: old row valid_to=now_T1; new row valid_from=now_T1 NULL valid_to. Codified D.22.1.

Final layout: 7-tile compact KEY PARAMETERS strip (REGIME + NET DEALER γ + SPOT CONTEXT + FLIP LEVEL + MAX γ STRIKE + PIN ZONE + ACCEL ZONE) → Positioning Landscape full-width with rollup row → Max Pain stacked full-width with rollup row (stacked NOT side-by-side per D.22.3 — vertical strike-axis alignment for cross-reading) → Pin Risk Score / Pin Probability / ATM Straddle 3-col row → Pin Risk Timeline → WCB / Market Breadth / India VIX / IV Skew 4-col Breadth & Volatility row → ICT Zones nearest-10 list → Signals stream. Mockup rendered to PNG via wkhtmltoimage (`marketview_v4_mockup.html` + `marketview_v4_render.png`).

### Phase-by-phase summary

**Phase 0 — Backend Supabase ALTER (P1 carry-forward primary mandate):** Lovable auto-scaffolded `merdian_parameters` mid-session with typed-column schema (NOT operator's planned single-jsonb); operator inspected via `information_schema.columns` paste; trimmed ALTER applied adding constraints + indexes + 3 STABLE read RPCs + 1 SECURITY DEFINER write RPC + `v_merdian_parameter_audit` view; RLS triplets applied to 8 base tables + 5 views.

**Phase 1 — Lovable frontend ship (6 iteration turns):** Turn 1 wrong-template discarded; Turn 2 SPA conversion `72dc296`; Turn 3 Supabase client + `.env` to public repo `6b95ded`; Turn 4 data wiring with 3 schema adaptations `2998819`; Turn 5 polish 6 fixes; Turn 6 final polish (strike-grid ticks + scroll-zoom/drag-pan/r-reset + ATM straddle VRD-style).

**Phase 2 — AWS Marketview hosting bootstrap:** `setup_marketview_aws_host.sh` installed nginx 1.18.0 + Node 20.20.2 + git, cloned repo, vite build, published `dist/` → `/var/www/marketview/`, nginx site config with SPA fallback + 30d cache + /_health endpoint, redeploy script.

**Phase 3 — AWS networking debug arc:** Browser connectivity failed for hours despite clean VPC/NACL/iptables; IMDSv2 token query revealed attached SG was `launch-wizard-1` not the operator-edited `launch-wizard-2` (orphan); adding TCP 80 to `launch-wizard-1` produced instant connectivity; TD-S39-NEW-4 filed.

**Phase 4 — CRITICAL SECURITY remediation:** Anon-grants audit post-RLS-triplet returned 91 rows = 7 privilege types × 13 surfaces (Lovable auto-grant had granted anon ALL privileges); remediated same-session via PL/pgSQL DO block REVOKE ALL + GRANT SELECT; post-remediation 13 rows all SELECT; TD-S39-NEW-1 S2 REMEDIATED; codified D.21.1.

**Phase 5 — Browser verification:** Live data rendering at `http://13.63.27.85/marketview` confirmed across NIFTY + SENSEX tabs — strike-grid ticks at correct intervals (50pt NIFTY / 100pt SENSEX), interactive chart, ATM straddle VRD-style, dealer flow scenarios, ICT nearest-10 zones, today's signals stream with entry_quality color chips, postmarket session label.

**Phase 6 — Doc-close (8 canonical files):** session_log.md S39 prepended; tech_debt.md 5 new TD-S39-NEW-* prepended above TD-S38-NEW-1 Active; MERDIAN_Decision_Index.md footer maintenance note S38 → S39 (no new ADRs); MERDIAN_Assumption_Register.md §D.21 added with 4 rows + footer S38 → S39; MERDIAN_Enhancement_Register.md Scope row bumped to ENH-01..ENH-112 + Part 4 detail blocks for ENH-110 Phase 1 + ENH-83 added + Part 5 Change Log row + Last updated S36 → S39 prepended; merdian_reference.json v29 → v30; CLAUDE.md v1.28 → v1.29 with 5 S39 settled-decisions bullets; CURRENT.md S39 Last session block prepended + S38 demoted to Previous via header rename only content verbatim per Rule 7.

### What Session 37 did, in 10 bullets

**Phase 1 — ENH-80 v1 build (ADR-014 schema):** detector code extended via `patch_s37_enh80_writer.py` to produce per-strike GEX rows in new `gex_strike_snapshots` table. Initial schema (ADR-014) carried 16 columns including single `gamma` + 3 derived booleans (`is_local_max`, `is_flip_zone`, `is_pin_candidate_bool`). Cross-symbol smoke-fire PASS: NIFTY abs_diff=9.8e-11 Cr, SENSEX abs_diff=1.2e-14 Cr against total `gamma_metrics.net_gex`. Sign convention validated.

**Phase 2 — Quant escalation surfaces architectural defect:** post smoke-fire quant review of derived booleans showed 39% NIFTY / 20% SENSEX fire rates — near-zero information content. Concurrent finding: single `gamma` column collapses IV skew (NIFTY 24050 ATM `gamma_call=0.00164` vs `gamma_put=0.00234` = +43% PE-richer = put-skew regime).

**Phase 3 — ADR-015 supersedes ADR-014 same session:** schema v2 redesign drops `gamma` (replaced by `gamma_call`+`gamma_put`) + 3 derived booleans (derivations to SQL views, not write-layer columns); keeps 12-col minimum-sufficient-statistic. Schema migration TRUNCATE + ALTER (4 cols dropped, 2 added). `patch_s37_enh80_writer_v2.py` deployed with auto-refuse guard on v1 marker. Post-v2 smoke-fire re-validated.

**Phase 4 — ENH-81 SQL views:** three views materialize from `gex_strike_snapshots` — `v_gex_strike_pin_zone` (prominence-around-peak recursive CTE walking by strike-value, τ_pin=0.3 hardcoded with `// TAU_PIN — swap for ENH-83 lookup` marker per ADR-016 deferral), `v_gex_strike_accel_zone` (symmetric trough walk), `v_dealer_flow_sim` (six-scenario ±0.5/1/2% grid). 4/4 falsification gates PASS including direction-correctness on 12 dealer-flow scenarios.

**Phase 5 — ENH-81 v1 Pine overlay:** `generate_pine_overlay.py` extended via `patch_s37_enh81_pine_overlay.py` to fetch positioning landscape + render PIN/ACCEL boxes. Source 17,192 → patched 23,300 chars (+6,108). Deployed; TradingView confirmed NIFTY [24100, 24300] green PIN above spot + ACCEL [23800, 24000] red below.

**Phase 6 — ENH-81 v2 Pine overlay fixes:** v1 ergonomic issues surfaced — SENSEX label collision (ICT + pin/accel both at midpoint), single-strike PIN renders as zero-height line, insufficient X-position separation. v2 (`patch_s37_enh81_pine_overlay_v2.py`) ships single-strike widening ±0.1% with 50pt floor + zone-edge label anchoring (`style_label_lower_left` for PIN top / `style_label_upper_left` for ACCEL bottom) + `bar_index+90` X-offset. SENSEX single-strike now visible 154pt band.

**Phase 7 — ADR-016 PROPOSED build-deferred:** parameter calibration pattern with temporal-immutable `merdian_parameters` table + mandatory `change_reason` + dot-hierarchical keys + TTL-cached read API + CLI. Design surfaced 9 magic-number clusters. Operator decision: build deferred per operator until N grows enough for cohort-driven recalibration to become useful. ENH-81 views ship with `// TAU_PIN — swap for ENH-83 lookup` markers throughout for future mechanical plumb.

**Phase 8 — GEX-as-context-not-gate decision:** operator framing *"Meridian doesn't need anymore gates. It's already gating everything."* — 5 existing gating layers sufficient (ADR-001 stability+validity, ENH-55 falsified env-disabled, routing-data-driven SKIP for BEAR_FVG, proximity tiers T1/T2/T3, ADR-009 graduated-strictness holdout). ENH-80/81 ship as display layer only (Lovable + Pine overlay); operator is integration layer. PE/CE GEX split preserved in schema but not surfaced — research-grade only.

**Phase 9 — Lovable.ai dashboard live:** three sequenced Lovable prompts produced dashboard at `lovable.dev/projects/e8fde6f9-58d0-4444-860d-508b3635b014` with NIFTY/SENSEX tabs, REGIME card, total GEX exposure, GEX-by-strike histogram with PIN/ACCEL ReferenceArea bands, summary strip, Hours-to-expiry fix. Per-table RLS+GRANT triplet shipped for anon-read access; brittleness surfaced (TD-S37-03 — silent empty datasets on RLS misconfiguration).

**Phase 10 — 7-canonical-file doc-close pack:** `MERDIAN_Decision_Index.md` 106→112 lines (ADR rows prepended) + `CLAUDE.md` v1.26→v1.27 (6 settled-decisions bullets + footer) + `CURRENT.md` (S37 prepend + S36 demote) + `session_log.md` 1118→1119 lines (S37 one-liner prepend) + `tech_debt.md` 2286→2328 lines (3 TD-S37-* + footer S37 block) + `MERDIAN_Assumption_Register.md` 491→518 lines (§D.19 + footer S37) + `merdian_reference.json` v27→v28. 3 new ADR files: ADR-014 + ADR-015 + ADR-016. Full-file no-crunch discipline maintained throughout.

### Critical lessons Session 37

(a) **Minimum-sufficient-statistic at write layer is the canonical schema design pattern when derivations are regime-conditional** — ADR-014→ADR-015 same-session supersession surfaced that derived booleans fire on 39%/20% of rows = near-zero information content; derivations belong in SQL views read at query time, not in columns stored at write time. Generalizes beyond GEX schema.

(b) **IV skew evidence is material and must be preserved in schema** — `gamma_call`/`gamma_put` split costs one column but preserves regime classification capability; collapsing to single `gamma` destroys put-skew vs call-skew discriminability.

(c) **Same-session ADR supersession is a valid pattern when quant review surfaces architectural defect post smoke-fire** — TRUNCATE + ALTER + redeploy is cheaper than shipping v1 + planning v2 migration, IFF no consumer code has locked against v1 yet. v1 patch trail + backup preserved for git audit.

(d) **GEX-as-context-not-gate framing** — operator's explicit *"Meridian doesn't need anymore gates"* rejection of gate-mode integration is settled architectural decision; ENH-80/81 ship as display layer only, operator is integration layer; this inverts the default assumption that every new signal becomes a gate.

(e) **Calibration-deferred-by-design pattern** — ADR-016 PROPOSED with build deferred until N grows; ENH-81 views ship with hardcoded τ=0.3 + inline `// TAU_PIN — swap for ENH-83 lookup` markers at every site; the marker pattern is the discipline that prevents τ from drifting into magic-number territory while keeping the calibration build queued mechanically.

(f) **Pine v6 visual disambiguation patterns** — label anchor points at zone edges (`style_label_lower_left`/`style_label_upper_left`) + X-offset prevent collision with ICT-layer labels; single-strike degeneracy resolved via ±0.1% widening with 50pt floor; both generalizable to any Pine box rendering of empirically-degenerate ranges.

(g) **Lovable per-table RLS pattern** — anon-read access requires `ALTER TABLE ... ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY` + `CREATE POLICY ... FOR SELECT TO anon USING (true)` + `GRANT SELECT ... TO anon` three-line canonical pattern; brittleness is RLS misconfiguration produces silent empty datasets not auth errors; document the exact RLS triplet inline in commit message + smoke-test via direct anon-key probe before deploying.

### What Session 36 did, in 10 bullets

**Phase 1 — Architectural framing review:** practitioner gamma-dashboard analysis (15+ screenshots of successful options writer's live cockpit holding ~18L profit via short 24000 PE + long 24000 PE June + short call ladder + put ratio credit spread) mapped to MERDIAN's ENH-80/81/82 build plan + Pin Risk Score continuous-0-100 transformation of ADR-002 v2 binary PINNED state. Layer 1 (data integrity) ENH list cataloged as blockers B1-B11; S36 targets B1 (gamma_metrics regression) + B10 (Dhan 429).

**Phase 2 — TD-S30-CANDIDATE-1 closure (writer-state-first diagnosis):** direct read of writer function body in first turn confirmed `/1e7` Cr conversion intact at S27 commit `241f943`; three-epoch SQL revealed historical data unit-mix (pre-S27 raw-rupees window from 2026-03-02 → 2026-05-04) not live regression. **The live writer was NEVER regressed; the residual was historical contamination mis-labeled at S29 close.** 7 sessions of carry-forward (S29 → S35) wasted by inverting the diagnosis order. Resolution: `backfill_gamma_metrics_to_main.py --mode overwrite` recovered March epoch (2,850 cycles); April-early-May ~4,300 rows DELETEd as confirmed gaps under TD-S35-NEW-1 chain coverage residual. **TD-S30-CANDIDATE-1 CLOSED-MISDIAGNOSIS.**

**Phase 3 — TD-080 / ENH-99 failure-shape diagnosis:** `script_execution_log` queried by (exit_reason, error_message, error_code) revealed three independent failure modes. Mode A 429 quota storm (recurring post-S29); Mode B 401 token expiry (SOLVED upstream S29 via `pull_token_from_supabase.py` atomic write + `dhan_token_probe_log` — zero post-S29 401s in 11 instrumented days); Mode C orphan RUNNING rows (25 stale, never reaped, audit-blind). **Mode B DROPPED from S36 scope.** Codified as engineering pattern §D.18.2: instrument the failure log before extending the retry layer.

**Phase 4 — ENH-99 Component 1 (`gamma_engine_retry_utils.retry_call` predicate):** patched via 3-iteration cycle. v1 abandoned at dry-run RETRY_UTILS anchor failure (CRLF/LF straddle in literal anchor); v2 INGEST + JANITOR APPLIED live, RETRY_UTILS still failed deep mismatch; v3 regex-anchor `def retry_call\(.*?raise RuntimeError\([^)]*\)` with re.DOTALL APPLIED clean (947 matched chars). New kwarg `retry_predicate: Callable[[Exception], bool] | None = None` + per-attempt evaluation + `[RETRY_BURN_DOWN]` stderr telemetry. Backwards-compatible.

**Phase 5 — ENH-99 Component 1 call-site patches:** `ingest_option_chain_local.py` 2 Dhan retry sites at lines 316 + 346 bumped to `attempts=6, delay=15.0, backoff_multiplier=1.5, retry_predicate=is_dhan_429`. ~24s → ~96s budget vs ~60s Dhan quota window. Local `is_dhan_429(exc)` predicate definition checks status 429 OR string-match on 'too many requests' / '805' in repr. Dhan 401s intentionally NOT matched (Mode B is solved upstream).

**Phase 6 — ENH-99 Component 2 (`orphan_run_janitor.py`):** NEW Local file produced through 3-iteration discovery cycle. v1 supabase-py KeyError on `SUPABASE_KEY` (house convention is `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` + raw HTTP per `ingest_option_chain_local.py`); v2 raw HTTP but `Prefer: return=representation` 400 from PostgREST (codified §D.18.3 — RLS interaction); v3 dropped Prefer + per-row error tolerance + body printing APPLIED. Smoke-fire test closed 22/24 orphans cleanly; 2 stragglers threw PG int4 overflow (orphan ages > ~24 days exceed `2^31 - 1`); int4 clamp added (codified §D.18.4); 2 stragglers closed via REPL with clamped duration. Final state 0 RUNNING > 5 min.

**Phase 7 — `MERDIAN_Orphan_Janitor` Task Scheduler registration:** weekly Mon-Fri 09:14 IST via PowerShell `Register-ScheduledTask` (Hidden + IgnoreNew + 5min execution limit + battery flags + Interactive Limited principal — same conventions as 19 other MERDIAN_* tasks established S29). Smoke-fire test 2026-05-25 17:26:26 `LastTaskResult=0`. **Task count 19 → 20.**

**Phase 8 — §D.18 codification:** 4 rows added to Assumption Register. D.18.1 writer-state-vs-data-state diagnosis ordering (foundational methodology rule from TD-S30-CANDIDATE-1 7-session-cost lesson). D.18.2 capture-layer Mode A/B/C taxonomy with Mode B SOLVED upstream (instrument-failure-log-before-retry-extension pattern). D.18.3 PostgREST `Prefer: return=representation` interacts with RLS on PATCH path differently than read path. D.18.4 `script_execution_log.duration_ms` is int4 — orphan durations > ~24 days must be clamped at write time.

**Phase 9 — TD filings:** 4 new TDs filed pending S37+. TD-S36-NEW-1 S3 gamma_metrics Apr-early-May row gap (closeable in ADR-013 Breeze fallback cycle). TD-S36-NEW-2 S3 `MERDIAN_Dhan_Token_Refresh` not instrumented to `script_execution_log` (30-min retrofit). TD-S36-NEW-3 S4 `dhan_token_probe_log` forward-only from 2026-05-10 (documentation-only gap). TD-S36-NEW-4 S3 `script_execution_log.duration_ms` int4 (clamp pattern works, int8 migration is proper fix).

**Phase 10 — Doc Protocol v4 Rule 3 close:** 9 canonical files updated full-file no-crunch (6 strict + 3 supplementary). MERDIAN_Decision_Index.md UNCHANGED (no new ADR S36). MD5 verified byte-identical Local + MERDIAN; AST parses. **Two flight-bugs surfaced + fixed:** (a) HOCS `run_id` is NOT NULL — v1/v2 silently failed all INSERTs while logging "wrote N rows" lies (supabase-py wraps the failure in try/except but the local accumulator was not rolled back); v3 generates one `RUN_ID = str(uuid.uuid4())` per invocation + logs run_id at start + insert-success log reflects actual rows inserted not the lying accumulator; `fill_2026_04_16_breeze_v3.py` md5 `5eae3849776ec2a6061ed2100ecb0e13`. Post-Breeze single-day recompute 2026-04-15→04-17 inserted 10 outcomes; verification on 6 zone-primitive retests 2026-04-16 shows all populated with plausible PnL (NIFTY H BEAR_FVG pnl_eod=-13.9%; SENSEX M5 BEAR_FVG @04:18 pnl_eod=+134%; SENSEX H BEAR_FVG pnl_eod=-100% — DTE=0 expired worthless; 4 level primitives correctly NULL). **ADR-012 SL writer extension (v9) shipped** via `patch_s35_adr012_v9_sl_writer.py` (4 edits, marker `ADR-012 (S35) v9`) + DDL `sql/20260524_adr012_v9_sl_columns.sql`: new constant `SL_BUFFER_PCT_DEFAULT = 0.005` (ADR-012 §3 default 50bps); 5 columns added to `ict_primitive_outcomes` (`sl_level` BULL=zone_low×(1−X) / BEAR=zone_high×(1+X); `sl_buffer_pct` 0.005 default; `sl_triggered_ts` first 5m bucket close-through after retest; `sl_exit_prem` held-strike premium at trigger; `pnl_with_sl_pct` (sl_exit_prem−entry_prem)/entry_prem×100); SL evaluation block in `compute_retest_atm_pnl` after existing EOD horizon loop (walks 5m clock-aligned bars from `first_retest_ts + 5min` through 15:25 IST EOD bucket close, aggregating from `bars_1m` once per session via cached `atm_cache["bars_5m_for_sl"]`); SL trigger lookups use SAME v8 prefetched chain cache (no new DB round-trips); plumbing through `upsert_outcomes`. Level primitives skip SL block by design; `pnl_with_sl_pct` degenerates to `option_pnl_eod` when SL never triggers intra-session. AST-validated pre+post; backup `build_ict_primitives_PRE_S35_v9.py`. **Single-cell verification 2026-05-14 NIFTY M5 (n=5 fresh rows after DELETE since writer is INSERT-only per TD-S35-NEW-4):** SL math byte-correct (BEAR zone_high=23562.8 × 1.005 = 23680.61); **2 BEAR primitives triggered SL** and exited 13-14pp better than held-to-EOD (BEAR_FVG 04:16: pnl_with_sl=-35.4% vs held=-48.4%; BEAR_FVG 05:48: -38.8% vs -53.4%); **3 BULL no-trigger correctly degenerated `pnl_with_sl_pct = option_pnl_eod`** (10.0 / -16.7 / -25.8%). ADR-012 hypothesis directionally evident on n=2 BEAR triggers; full validation cohort (n=65 W+D+H zone retest clears ADR-012 §3 n≥50 threshold) deferred to S36 TRUNCATE + full recompute since v9 writer is INSERT-only. **TD-S35-NEW-4 S3 filed** for INSERT-only-on-schema-add writer limitation. **§D.17 added to Assumption Register** with 4 rows D.17.1-D.17.4 codifying the four S35 findings (dual-source chain reader VALIDATED; HOCS strike-coverage structural limit VALIDATED → TD-S35-NEW-1; Breeze full-chain capability VALIDATED → ADR-013 PROPOSED + ENH-109 PROPOSED; ADR-012 SL writer integration VALIDATED on n=5 single-cell). **ADR-013 PROPOSED** (Breeze ICICI Direct API as canonical historical options backfill source — full-chain capability with no ATM±N cap; 3-year lookback / 5000 calls/day / 100/min throttle / SEBI static-IP whitelist; SENSEX `BSESEN/BFO` symbology; linked to ENH-109). **ENH-109 PROPOSED** (graduate Breeze rollingoption + get_historical_data_v2 as canonical historical backfill — replaces vendor renewal + S22 Kite + Dhan rollingoption ATM±10 cap; defers vendor renewal dependency; Phase 3 GEX time-series prerequisite per ADR-002 v2). **0 git commits / 0 tags this session** (`session-35-close` pending operator). **10 canonical files modified at session close per Doc Protocol v4 Rule 3 + Rule 9 + Rule 10 + Rule 11 — no-crunch / no-append discipline maintained throughout: 7 strict canonical (`CLAUDE.md` v1.24→v1.25 + `CURRENT.md` + `session_log.md` + `tech_debt.md` 4 new TDs + `MERDIAN_Decision_Index.md` ADR-012 IMPLEMENTED + ADR-013 PROPOSED + `MERDIAN_Assumption_Register.md` §D.17 + `merdian_reference.json` v25→v26) + 3 supplementary (`MERDIAN_Enhancement_Register.md` ENH-109 entry, `MERDIAN_Deployment_Topology.md` Breeze MALPHA-analog catalog + MERDIAN AWS instance ID drift annotation, `MERDIAN_System_Map.md` HOCS table inventory).** |

### What Session 35 did, in 10 bullets

**Phase 1 — Direct DB diagnostic surfaced the tier-transition architecture within first turn:** SQL on `hist_option_bars_1m` vs `historical_option_chain_snapshots` (HOCS) confirmed pre-Apr-2026 vendor / post-Apr-2026 MERDIAN-ingest split sharing a 2026-04-01 UTC boundary; calendar clean overlap; HOCS keyed on `symbol` text / `ltp` not `close` / 5-min cadence vs vendor 1-min. Operator's S34 framing validated.

**Phase 2 — ENH-106 v8 dual-source reader patch deployed:** 8 edits to `build_ict_primitives.py`; new `CHAIN_TIER_BOUNDARY_UTC = 2026-04-01` constant + `_source_tier()` + `_prefetch_hocs_for_tuple()` helpers + per-tuple boundary-split routing + `option_pnl_source TEXT` audit column. AST-validated pre+post; backup preserved.

**Phase 3 — v8.1 calendar fix + v8.2 RPC swap:** Single-cell test on 2026-05-14 NIFTY M5 surfaced `n_tuples == 0` because `_load_expiry_calendar` only queried vendor side (caps 2026-04-07). v8.1 UNIONs HOCS expiries via paginated SELECT DISTINCT — hung 15 min on 2.67M-row scan + PostgREST 8s timeout. v8.2 swapped pagination for RPC `get_hocs_distinct_expiries(text)` STABLE function + `(symbol, expiry_date)` covering index; 325ms EXPLAIN ANALYZE.

**Phase 4 — Full TRUNCATE + recompute 19,571 outcomes in 2,107s:** NIFTY 8,925 / SENSEX 10,646; 2,773 (strike, expiry, type) tuples; 1.72M pre bars + 49,204 post cycles; boundary routing clean per `option_pnl_source` audit (13,220 vendor + 1,851 merdian + 4,500 NULL).

**Phase 5 — TD-S34-NEW-4 closure analysis:** 317/541 post-Apr retests recovered to non-NULL option_pnl_*. Diagnostic 4-lens partition attributed residual 224 NULLs: 132 architecturally-exempt level primitives (PDH/PDL/PWH/PWL/PMH/PML — direction=NONE); 14 single-day gap 2026-04-16; ~75 HOCS strike-coverage misses. Zone-primitive denominator recovery 317/409 = 78% mechanical.

**Phase 6 — Breeze surgical fill of 2026-04-16 from MERDIAN AWS via SSM:** instance `i-0878c118835386ec2`; static EIP `13.63.27.85` registered with SEBI mandatory IP-whitelist on Breeze portal app "Meridian"; daily session token via 2FA browser flow + portal app-key/secret. File transfer via multi-line nano paste (after base64 + chunked-paste failures via SSM); MD5 byte-verified.

**Phase 7 — Two flight-bugs surfaced and fixed:** (a) HOCS `run_id` NOT NULL; v1/v2 silently failed INSERTs while logging "wrote N rows" lies; v3 uses `RUN_ID = str(uuid.uuid4())` per invocation + real-rows-only success log. (b) SENSEX `stock_code="BSESEN"` not "SENSEX" — empirical 6-variant probe identified the working value; not in Breeze public docs.

**Phase 8 — Final Breeze write: 107,630 HOCS rows source=`breeze_backfill_s35`:** NIFTY 61,899 + SENSEX 45,731; 3 expiries per symbol × 2 OT × 31 strikes; far-OTM tapering on far-monthly expiries. Post-Breeze recompute on 2026-04-15→04-17 populated 6 zone-primitive retests with plausible PnL; **TD-S34-NEW-4 CLOSED-MECHANICAL** with 331/409 = 81% zone-primitive recovery + structural residual to TD-S35-NEW-1.

**Phase 9 — ADR-012 SL writer extension v9 shipped + n=5 single-cell verified:** 5 sl_* columns + SL_BUFFER_PCT_DEFAULT 0.005 + SL evaluation block in `compute_retest_atm_pnl` walking 5m bars from retest_5m+5min through 15:25 IST EOD; SL trigger lookups reuse v8 chain cache (zero new DB round-trips). SL math byte-correct: 2 BEAR primitives triggered and exited 13-14pp better than held-to-EOD; 3 BULL no-trigger correctly degenerated to `option_pnl_eod`. Writer INSERT-only on outcomes surfaced as TD-S35-NEW-4.

**Phase 10 — 10-canonical-file doc-close pack per Doc Protocol v4 Rule 3 + Rule 9 + Rule 10 + Rule 11:** 7 strict canonical (CLAUDE.md v1.25 + CURRENT.md + session_log.md + tech_debt.md +73 lines / 4 new TDs + Decision Index ADR-012 IMPLEMENTED + ADR-013 PROPOSED + Assumption Register §D.17 + reference.json v26) + 3 supplementary (Enhancement Register ENH-109 + Topology Breeze MALPHA-analog + System Map HOCS inventory). Full-file no-crunch discipline maintained; targeted file-edit operations preserve byte-identical content outside insertion anchors.

After: bar_ts is true UTC."; line 203 `normalize_hist_bar_ts()` era-aware helper; line 785 `_vendor_bar_ts_label()` for chain DB filtering) confirmed all prior research (D-FVG retest 78-86% WR, H-FVG retest 60-76% WR, ENH-100 magnitude, ADR-009 holdout splits) is uncontaminated by TZ era boundary. **Pivot to universal big-move-day audit** at operator direction. Parity threshold both indices ≥1.0% intraday from session open over 2025-04-01→2026-05-19 → 119 days (NIFTY 31 DOWN + 26 UP = 57 of 279 trading days = 20.4%; SENSEX 33 DOWN + 29 UP = 62 of 278 = 22.3%) via era-aware session-bars CTE on `hist_spot_bars_5m`. **Capture audit:** for each ≥1% move-day, find highest-priority aligned MERDIAN primitive (BEAR for DOWN / BULL for UP) that formed before move-day AND whose zone interacted with price (zone_low ≤ day_high AND zone_high ≥ day_open); status IN ('ACTIVE','MITIGATED'); ROW_NUMBER over (PARTITION BY symbol, d ORDER BY interacted DESC, tf_rank DESC, source_bar_ts DESC) WHERE rk=1. **Result: 118/119 captured (99.2%).** One miss: NIFTY 2025-05-20 DOWN -1.32% — D DISPLACEMENT_DOWN existed but ALIGNED_BUT_NO_INTERACTION (price didn't reach zone). **Origin structure breakdown (n=118):** BEAR_FVG 56 (47%) / BULL_FVG 43 (36%) / BULL_OB 12 (10%) / BEAR_OB 7 (6%) — FVG dominates 84% of origins; D 56 (47%) / W 32 (27%) / H 17 (14%) / M5 13 (11%) — D and W combine 74%. **Standout zone-reuse:** 2026-04-06 BULL_FVG W served as origin for 4 separate ≥1% UP days (Apr 7, Apr 13, May 14, May 18); 2025-04-04 BEAR_FVG D fired on March 2026 crash days NIFTY+SENSEX 03-23/24 (~354 days old); 2025-04-15 BULL_FVG W triggered 5 reactions. **Implication: MERDIAN's ICT primitive layer sees every ≥1% move structurally; capture is not the binding constraint on trade discoverability — selection is.** **Selection problem articulated:** on any given morning 50+ active aligned primitives exist across W/D/H/M5; current system has no ranking layer to predict which fires today. Selection-research arc proposed as 3-5 session work item with five candidate features: pre-open structural signature (gap + multi-TF aligned + sweep); same-day momentum confirmation gate (first H bar close direction); HTF context alignment (require W direction alignment for D zones); zone freshness (first-touch > N-touch retest hit rate); DTE-aware option leg selection (extends S33 DTE 3-bucket finding). ENH-108 N-touch retest detection identified as foundational schema unlock — ADR-004 §10 records only `first_retest_ts`, missing the 112 invisible-retest move-days powering the captured cohort. **PnL quantification on retest cohort:** 22-row retest backtest assembled from `ict_primitive_outcomes.first_retest_ts` falling on ≥1% move-day via VALUES-cohort SQL pattern; 15 rows lost to TD-S34-NEW-4 chain coverage gap (all post-Apr-2026 dates returned zero rows from `hist_option_bars_1m`); usable cohort = 7. **All 7 directionally correct** (entry at retest moment, long ATM CE for UP / PE for DOWN, NIFTY lot 75 / SENSEX lot 20; entry strikes manually picked via ROUND(spot/grid)*grid where grid=50 NIFTY / 100 SENSEX; nearest weekly expiry via MIN(expiry_date) BETWEEN d AND d + INTERVAL '10 days'). **Held-to-EOD total: ₹106,888** (NIFTY 1162.65 premium points × 75 lot = ₹87,266; SENSEX 981.10 × 20 lot = ₹19,622). **SL variant backtest on the 7:** intra-bar 5% wick → 0/7 winners mean -8.13 pts; 10% wick → 0/7 mean -16.30; 15% wick → 3/7 mean +197.66; 1m-close-through 5%/10% → 0/3. **Spot-anchored 5m-close-through at 0.3%/0.5%/0.8% adverse: 0/0/0 SL triggers; 7/7 winners at every level.** Tightest spot SL (0.3%) never triggered on any of the 7 — once price has tagged the zone and begun rejecting, it does not return through within the same-day window. Premium wicked 5-15% on the same trades from microstructure alone (bid-ask, theta on tight DTE, IV crush as morning gamma compresses) uncorrelated with thesis. **ADR-012 ACCEPTED:** spot-anchored stop-loss doctrine for ICT retest entries (BEAR retest stopped when 5m spot bar closes ≥ zone_high * (1+X); BULL stopped when closes ≤ zone_low * (1-X); X = 0.5% provisional default; consistent with ADR-004 §10 breach rule template close-through-not-wick). Premium SL on ATM held strikes formalized as wrong instrument-stop pairing. Time-based exit policy (ENH-107) composes orthogonally. Implementation pending future session. **TD-S34-NEW-4 FILED (S2):** `hist_option_bars_1m` post-2026-04-01 coverage gap. **Operator-confirmed root cause:** pre-Apr-2026 chain is vendor-purchased and dense; post-Apr-2026 chain is MERDIAN-ingested via a different writer path. The "MERDIAN failed to ingest entirely" hypothesis cannot be the full picture — plenty of full-ingestion days post-Apr-2026 observed elsewhere. ### What Session 34 did, in 10 bullets

**Phase 1 — S33 carry-forward pivot (operator-directed):** S33 P0_PRIMARY was D-TF horizon extension via `mfe_pct` + `time_to_mfe_min` analysis (TD-S33-NEW-4). Early SQL surfaced "time_to_mfe_min p90 = 25-30 min on every cell" — MFE search window appears capped at ~30 min. Operator redirected to universal big-move-day audit; D-TF analysis remains S35+ carry-forward.

**Phase 2 — TZ artifact / mixed-resolution diagnostic on hist_spot_bars_1m:** Table returned 60-bar/day historical SENSEX (~6m), 53-bar NIFTY (~7m), 375-bar real 1m post-Apr-2026 — mixed-resolution + broken NIFTY pre-Apr-2026 coverage. Initial "sparse data" framing operator-rejected; pivoted to canonical `hist_spot_bars_5m` 41,248 rows full year with era-aware time handling.

**Phase 3 — Research-validity audit:** Operator challenged whether prior research stood given TZ bug. Audit of `build_ict_primitives.py` (IST constant, era-boundary comment, normalize_hist_bar_ts helper, `_vendor_bar_ts_label` for chain DB filtering) confirmed all prior research is uncontaminated by TZ era boundary. Era-aware time handling is canonical.

**Phase 4 — Universal big-move-day capture audit:** Parity threshold both indices ≥1.0% intraday over 2025-04-01→2026-05-19 → 119 days. Highest-priority aligned MERDIAN primitive picked by tf_rank (W=4 > D=3 > H=2 > M5=1) then most recent.

**Phase 5 — Capture result + origin distribution:** **118/119 captured (99.2%)** — one miss NIFTY 2025-05-20 ALIGNED_BUT_NO_INTERACTION. Origin distribution: FVG 84% / OB 16%; D+W 74% / H 14% / M5 11%. Standout zone-reuse: W BULL_FVG 2026-04-06 fired 4 UP days; D BEAR_FVG 2025-04-04 fired March 2026 crash days (~354 days old).

**Phase 6 — Selection problem articulated:** 50+ active aligned primitives every morning; system has no ranking layer. Five candidate selection features identified. Selection-research arc framed as 3-5 session work item; framework doc deferred to S35+.

**Phase 7 — Retest cohort PnL backtest:** 22-row cohort → 15 lost to TD-S34-NEW-4 chain coverage gap → usable n=7. All 7 directionally correct. Held-to-EOD +₹106,888 on 1 lot (NIFTY ₹87,266 + SENSEX ₹19,622).

**Phase 8 — SL doctrine empirical foundation:** Premium SL 5%/10% → 0/7 winners; 15% → 3/7; 1m-close-through 5%/10% → 0/3. Spot SL 0.3%/0.5%/0.8% adverse 5m-close → **0/0/0 SL triggers; 7/7 winners at every level**. Microstructure noise (bid-ask, theta, IV crush) routinely consumes 5-15% on first-30min wicks uncorrelated with thesis.

**Phase 9 — ADR-012 + ENH-108 + TD-S34-NEW-4 filed:** ADR-012 ACCEPTED (141 lines / 12565 bytes). ENH-108 PROPOSED — `ict_primitive_touches` table recommendation; foundational for selection research. TD-S34-NEW-4 FILED S2 — operator-corrected root cause framing as vendor → MERDIAN-ingest tier transition.

### What Session 33 did, in 10 bullets

**Phase 1 — Mid-session ENH-103 ship (before architectural pivot):**

- ENH-103 retest-anchored option PnL — 5 columns `option_pnl_5m/15m/30m/60m/eod_pct` added to `ict_primitive_outcomes` via SQL migration; v6 writer extended `compute_retest_atm_pnl` to use `hist_atm_option_bars_5m` matching ENH-100 v3 source choice; backfill rebuilt outcomes ~5 min; cohort showed universally-negative medians across every (symbol, tf, primitive_type, direction) cell — same architectural error as ENH-100 v3, same diagnostic.

**Phase 2 — Operator-prompted architectural diagnosis (within one push-back cycle):**

- Initial framing "sparse vendor data" challenged by operator with verified knowledge — 12 months of chain data paid for and validated dense; challenge was correct. `hist_atm_option_bars_5m` is the 27k-row aggregated table built for **wick-reversal analysis** (read by `experiment_26/27/27b`), NOT for held-strike PnL across horizons. Same-strike enforcement against the aggregated table filters 50-70% of primitives where vendor rolled ATM — non-random self-selection against winners. Experiments 1-50 made the inverse error (no same-strike check on rolling-ATM source → inflated coverage but mathematically wrong). **Canonical source is `hist_option_bars_1m` chain (54.8M rows, dense, paid-for)** with manual ATM strike picking via `STRIKE_INTERVAL` constant (NIFTY/50, SENSEX/100) + held strike across horizons.

**Phase 3 — ENH-106 v7 writer patch + backfill:**

- Patch `patch_s33_enh106_chain_heldstrike_atm_pnl_writer.py` deployed (4 substitutions in `build_ict_primitives.py`): SUB1 head of `compute_atm_pnl_and_dte` (chain-cache + early return); SUB2 `compute_retest_atm_pnl` full body; SUB3 4 new helpers inserted before `compute_outcomes`; SUB4 `compute_outcomes` head calls prefetch before per-primitive loop. Marker `ENH-106 (S33) v7`. AST validated pre+post; backup `build_ict_primitives_PRE_S33_v7.py` preserved. Per-tuple range-prefetch architecture: 2,256 unique (strike, expiry, type) tuples × 1 paginated query each over [min_ts, max_ts+1min) caches ~1.67M chain bars in ~10 min/symbol; empirical expiry calendar via DISTINCT on `hist_atm_option_bars_5m.expiry_date` handles NSE/BSE 2025-09-01 weekday swap + ~15% holiday-shifted weeks + same-week double expiries.
- TRUNCATE `ict_primitive_outcomes` + full re-backfill 1775.9s rebuilt 19,399 outcomes (NIFTY 8838 + SENSEX 10561). NIFTY: 839 tuples / 884 retests / 704,272 chain bars prefetched 830.7s. SENSEX: 1417 tuples / 1023 retests / 970,904 bars 656.3s.

**Phase 4 — Cohort flip empirically validates rebuild:**

- Coverage jumped 20-44× on populated M5 cells (NIFTY M5 BEAR 85→2650; SENSEX M5 BULL 60→2662). Median PnL flipped universally NEGATIVE (v6) → POSITIVE on every directional cell with real spot edge: NIFTY M5 BULL_OB median 30m +17.2% / WR 82.1% / N=28; SENSEX M5 BULL_OB +16.4% / 77.8% / N=45; NIFTY M5 DISPLACEMENT_DOWN +14.8% / 77.4% / N=93; NIFTY H DISPLACEMENT_DOWN +34.7% / 100% / N=17. M5 FVGs remain coin-flips (~50% WR, ~0% median 30m) — confirms D.14.2 independent of source-table.

**Phase 5 — Retest cohort empirically validates ADR-009 §Phase 1 cross-symbol:**

- NIFTY D BULL_FVG retest median 30m +11.7% / median 60m +22.3% / WR 88.2% / N=17 (strongest single retest cell); NIFTY H BEAR_FVG retest +4.8% / 7.3% / 72.5% / N=51; SENSEX H BEAR_FVG retest +9.9% / 6.3% / 75.6% / N=45; SENSEX H BULL_FVG retest +7.0% / 6.7% / 68.4% / N=38. Two independent metrics agreeing: spot-WR S31-B + option-PnL S33. D.14.1 strengthened.

**Phase 6 — M5 OB retest falsified at option-PnL level:**

- NIFTY M5 BEAR_OB retest median 30m -11.1% / WR 35.3% / N=17; SENSEX M5 BEAR_OB retest -5.1% / 43.5% / N=23; SENSEX M5 BULL_OB retest -4.3% / 47.8% / N=23. All M5 retest cells negative median across NIFTY+SENSEX. D.14.3 promoted from "investigation queued" to "falsified at option-PnL level." Trade M5 OBs at formation only.

**Phase 7 — DTE 3-bucket structure discovered:**

- DTE=0 feast-or-famine (NIFTY M5 DISPLACEMENT_UP median 30m +58.7%; SENSEX +36.2%; but DOWN-direction median 60m turns NEGATIVE -4.8% to -9.2% — exit at 30m mandatory). DTE=1-2 M5 sweet spot (NIFTY M5 BEAR_OB median 30m +24.4% / WR 80% / N=15; SENSEX M5 DISP_UP median 60m +38.3% / WR 83.3% / N=12). DTE≥3 H-TF home (NIFTY H DISP_DOWN median 60m +37.5% / WR 100% / N=12; SENSEX H DISP_UP median 60m +48.2% / WR 92.3% / N=13).

**Phase 8 — D-TF horizon hypothesis identified (carry-forward):**

- D-TF cells positive spot WR ~67% but negative option PnL median at 30m/60m — theta drains before spot move materializes. Hypothesis: D-TF needs horizons longer than 60m. `mfe_pct` + `time_to_mfe_min` columns may already answer "what horizon" via SQL-only analysis. Filed as TD-S33-NEW-4 S3.

**Phase 9 — Doc Protocol v4 Rule 10 mandatory ADR-011 filed:**

- ADR-011 (189 lines / 15440 bytes) Status: Accepted; supersedes ADR-010 v3 §"Source table choice" only (schema clauses unchanged). Decision: chain-table `hist_option_bars_1m` canonical for held-strike PnL with manual ATM picking + held strike across horizons. Six architectural properties documented (manual ATM picking via STRIKE_INTERVAL; empirical expiry calendar via DISTINCT; held strike across horizons; DTE derivation from picked expiry; era-aware vendor labeling; per-tuple range prefetch). Evidence: coverage lift + median flip + retest empirical confirmation of ADR-009 + M5 OB retest falsification + DTE structure discovery. 5 Alternatives rejected. Governance language one-liner provided.

**Phase 10 — 8-canonical-file + 1-new-ADR doc-close pack per Doc Protocol v4 Rule 3 + Rule 9 + Rule 10 + Rule 11:**

- ADR-011 NEW (189 lines / 15440 bytes); CLAUDE.md v1.22 → v1.23 (+43 lines / +11007 bytes); CURRENT.md (this file — S33 Last session block prepended; S31-B demoted to Previous session per no-crunch); session_log.md (+1 line / +15320 bytes — S33 paragraph prepended); tech_debt.md (+68 lines / +7692 bytes — 4 new TD-S33-NEW-* prepended); Decision Index (+2 lines / +3573 bytes — ADR-011 row prepended); Assumption Register (+11 lines / +5379 bytes — §D.15 4 rows); Enhancement Register (ENH-100/103/106 IMPLEMENTED status updates); merdian_reference.json (v23 → v24 changelog entry). **Project knowledge upload pending S34** (5-session carry-forward backlog).

### What Session 31-B did, in 12 bullets

**Build execution + sanity check:**

1. **Task 4 full-window backfill executed 2026-05-21 18:57 IST window 2025-04-01 → 2026-05-19 tfs=W,D,H,M5.** NIFTY 113,893 1m bars → 8,838 primitives + 8,838 outcomes (1:1 enforced via FK CASCADE); SENSEX 115,056 1m bars → 10,561 primitives + 10,561 outcomes (1:1); total 156.3s combined (53.7s + 102.6s). Per-symbol ~30s cost amortization informs ENH-100 re-compute baseline estimate.

2. **Q1 counts sanity check PASS.** Monotonic W<D<H<M5 per symbol confirmed healthy across both symbols. PDH=276-277 ≈ trading days; PWH/PWL=59 ≈ weeks; PMH/PML=13 ≈ months (period='M' filed under TF='W' per S31-A §10 schema enum mapping). FVG > OB at every TF (FVG dominates as expected — OB requires displacement candle following body). SWEEP_HIGH/SWEEP_LOW M5 dominant (NIFTY 3309/3345, SENSEX 4120/3939) — M5 sweep is the high-frequency signal class.

3. **Q2 WR sanity check (in-sample full window) surfaces OB retest paradox + retest-primary thesis for FVGs.** M5 FVG both sym both dir 48-51% formation + 51-55% retest baseline coin-flip standalone. M5 OB 77-87% formation + 47-58% retest — **formation > retest by 30-40pp, paradox documented as D.14.3** (entry on formation candle beats waiting for retest entry for OB patterns; opposite of FVG behavior). D/H FVG 56-68% formation + 71-88% retest — retest-primary thesis HOLDS for FVGs. Sweep M5 N>3k 61-63% real edge. Displacement M5 72-80% formation. **SENSEX H DISPLACEMENT_DOWN 34.6% vs NIFTY 62.2% directional anomaly worth investigation** (filed D.14.4).

**ADR-009 Phase-1 holdout validation:**

4. **ADR-009 Phase-1 holdout split executed** train 2025-04-01 → 2026-02-28 vs holdout 2026-03-01 → 2026-05-19 via FULL OUTER JOIN side-by-side SQL per (symbol, TF, primitive_type, mode). N≥30 per side filter applied. 10-month train / 2.5-month holdout meets ADR-009 Phase-1 graduated-strictness 67/33 split discipline at N≥60 per cell with 10pp tolerance.

5. **Headline finding: 4 buckets simultaneously HOLD + STRENGTHEN on holdout.** NIFTY H BEAR_FVG retest 75.0 → 85.2 (+10.2, N=29); NIFTY H BULL_FVG retest 64.3 → 90.0 (+25.7, N=27); SENSEX H BEAR_FVG retest 76.6 → 92.0 (+15.4, N=30); SENSEX H BULL_FVG retest 70.2 → 80.8 (+10.6, N=30). Deltas all in favorable direction (holdout exceeds train), opposite of overfit signature. **This single finding justifies the entire S31-B effort.** Codified as D.14.1 + ENH-102.

6. **What holds (delta ≤±5pp N≥30 both sides):** NIFTY H BEAR_FVG form +2.8; NIFTY H BULL_FVG form +2.1; NIFTY M5 DISPLACEMENT_DOWN -4.6; NIFTY M5 SWEEP_LOW -4.6; SENSEX M5 SWEEP_LOW -0.8; NIFTY M5 SWEEP_HIGH borderline -5.5. Sweeps hold modestly ~60% across the board; useful as context filter not standalone.

7. **What collapsed (overfit indicators):** M5 FVG both sym both dir form & retest collapse to 45-57% on holdout — at-or-below baseline; coin-flip confirmed; **standalone refuted as D.14.2**. SENSEX M5 BEAR_OB form 82.6→65.2 (-17.4 overfit, N=23 borderline). NIFTY H DISPLACEMENT_DOWN form 68.2→53.3 (-14.9 overfit). SENSEX H DISPLACEMENT_DOWN 38.7→28.6 (consistent reversal pattern across train + holdout — not edge in assumed direction; possibly inverse signal worth flipping; investigation D.14.4).

**Pine v6 visual overlay iteration + descope:**

8. **Pine v6 Task 5 descoped after 5-version iteration.** Built `MERDIAN_ICT_Primitives_canonical.pine` v1 472 lines through v5 537 lines mirroring Python detector logic verbatim with MTF rendering via `request.security` per TF. Six Pine v6 ergonomic walls hit across iterations: CE10243 declaration-statement (editor stale), descending for-loop requires `by -1`, CE10235 if/else type-compat (move label.new to standalone if no else), `close[1] + lookahead_off` double-shift bug, CE10088 `var int` global mutation requires `var array<int> = array.from(0)` wrapper, `max_boxes_count=500` hard cap silently GC's overflow boxes (mutations on GC'd boxes silently no-op). Diagnostic counter revealed Zones=1928 / Active=158 / Broken=1770 / Breach fires=1770 (mutation perfect) / Levels=0 (PDH/PDL fetch bug from double-shift). Final v5 canonical PDH/PDL idiom `[high[1], low[1]] + lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_on` works both same-TF and cross-TF; `showBroken=false` default to bypass GC silent-no-op trap.

9. **Operator descope decision:** "Its messed up. Lets drop the pine script for now and proceed with the rest." Task 5 deferred to wave 1.5 or later session with architectural design prerequisite (TF filtering for <500 zones, GC-aware rendering, alternative display patterns) not just code-and-paste. Filed as TD-S31B-NEW-1 S3.

**Doc-close pack:**

10. **8 canonical files updated per Doc Protocol v4 Rule 3 + Rule 9 session-end checklist.** Full file downloads no-crunch discipline maintained throughout. Enhancement Register (+143 lines net — 3 ENH detail blocks + 3 status table rows + header + scope); session_log.md (+1 line — S31-B paragraph prepended at line 1); CURRENT.md (this file — S31-B block prepended; S30 demoted to Previous session via header rename only, content preserved verbatim); tech_debt.md (TD-S31B-NEW-1 added to Active section); merdian_reference.json v22→v23 (change_log array + tables + files inventory + last_updated + JSON parses cleanly); Decision Index (ADR-004 IMPLEMENTED row prepended + Pending ADRs table updated); Assumption Register (§D.14 added with 5 rows D.14.1-D.14.5); CLAUDE.md v1.21→v1.22 (S31-B engineering discoveries section + Pine v6 ergonomic catalog + 4 settled-decisions; full v1.21→v1.1 history preserved verbatim).

11. **Three new ENHs filed PROPOSED at next-available IDs past ENH-99 reservation.** ENH-100 P0 (outcomes-magnitude profiling + ATM PnL + DTE — 13 columns + re-compute + ADR-010 schema extension at build time; gates ENH-101 + answers 6 operator follow-up questions); ENH-101 P1 BLOCKED-BY-ENH-100 (stop-loss optimization from MAE distribution — 90th pct of `mae_pct` among profitable trades per (symbol, TF, primitive_type, direction, retest_or_formation) cell with N≥30); ENH-102 P1 (H-FVG-retest signal isolation — codify ADR-009 Phase-1 holdout 4-bucket finding into live routing rule; `MERDIAN_ENH102_ENABLED` env flag default OFF; integration target S31-C consumer rewire). ENH-99 reservation for TD-080 Dhan 429 retry layer + circuit breaker explicitly preserved (S29/S30 carry-forward).

### Critical lessons Session 31-B

(a) **ADR-004 Wave 1 was the single largest end-to-end build in MERDIAN history** — 5 primitives × 2 symbols × 4 timeframes × 14-month window producing 19,399 primitives + 19,399 outcomes in 156.3s; build discipline (S31-A spec → Task 1 detector → Task 2 writer → Task 3 DDL → Task 4 backfill → Task 5 visual descoped) held throughout; ADR-009 Phase-1 holdout split as immediate validation produced the headline finding within the same session as the build.

(b) **Pine v6 ergonomic walls are systemic not incidental** — six independent classes of bugs surfaced in five iterations of one script: descending for-loop `by -1` requirement (silent zero-iterations), if/else type-compat CE10235 (compile-time), `var int` global mutation CE10088 (compile-time, array.from(0) workaround), `close[1] + lookahead_off` double-shift (silent wrong value), max_boxes_count=500 hard cap with silent GC of overflow boxes (mutations on GC'd boxes silently no-op), PDH/PDL canonical fetch idiom `[high[1], low[1]] + lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_on`; codified in CLAUDE.md as Pine v6 engineering catalog for future Pine work.

(c) **Pine v6 visual overlay is no longer a "quick task"** — Task 5 estimated as 0.5-1 session at S31-A planning grew to 5 iterations and operator descoped; the visual MTF-breach + max_boxes constraint requires architectural design (TF filtering, GC-aware rendering, alternative display patterns) not just code-and-paste. Estimate this class of task generously going forward.

(d) **Holdout-validation is non-negotiable per ADR-009 Phase 1.** S31-B's clean holdout split (10-month train / 2.5-month holdout, both with N≥30 per cell on H-FVG-retest buckets) produced a verdict that survives scrutiny — the headline finding is not a single-cohort artifact. The four buckets independently validate, deltas are large and in favorable direction. Compare to S29's Phase 0b verdict that was correct on its cohort but did not transfer to live cohort (S30 D.9.3 cohort-translation save) — S31-B's verdict has not yet been transfer-checked against `signal_snapshots` runtime cohort; ENH-102 deployment gated on D.13.1 pre-flight before flag flip.

(e) **Schema extensions (ENH-100 ADR-010) ship with ADR per Doc Protocol v4 Rule 10** — additive columns on research-tier table is lightweight ADR but discipline applies; the alternative of "skip ADR because it's just columns" is the failure mode v4 codified out of existence.

(f) **ENH-99 reservation preserved across three sessions** (S29 file → S30 preserve → S31-B explicit skip-and-document) — Doc Protocol v2 Rule 5 monotonic-no-reuse discipline applied correctly. ENH-99 remains reserved for TD-080 Dhan 429 retry layer + circuit breaker ENH spec.

### What Session 30 did, in 12 bullets

**Diagnostic (live cohort cohort-translation save + gate audit + OB attachment defect):**

1. **`s30_path1_live_cohort_pnl_v5.py` produced the live cohort empirical edge measurement.** Live `signal_snapshots` ICT-tagged 8-week cohort (2026-03-23 → 2026-05-15), gates-off filter (action derived from direction_bias before LONG_GAMMA / ENH-77 / ENH-88 / DTE / confidence overrides). N=211 setups; WR 58.3%; mean +6.96%; median +3.38%; pooled +1,469.13pp. BULL_FVG sub-cohort N=99 WR 58.6% (beats Compendium settled 50% with z=1.72 one-sided p=0.043); BEAR_FVG sub-cohort N=107 WR 58.9% (beats Compendium settled 46% with z=2.65 two-sided p=0.008); BULL_OB N=5 (does not replicate Compendium 84% at this N); BEAR_OB **N=0** (orthogonal OB attachment defect, see #4). SENSEX dominates cohort 123/211 = 58%; SENSEX BULL_FVG WR 64.2% mean +12.49%.

2. **v1-v5 cohort progression demonstrated D.9.3 cohort-translation discipline in action.** v1/v2 attempted `hist_atm_option_bars_5m` cohort but table ends 2026-03-30 pre-window. v3 used archive + live `option_chain_snapshots` routing (cutover 2026-05-04) — 56 of 81 setups enriched; median +0.47% POSITIVE on ICT cohort. v4 added persistence × P&L analysis — flipped-10-20m bucket BEST (WR 64.3% mean +4.00%) vs held-full-30m WORST (WR 50% mean -1.80%); T+30m exit timing past asymmetric-winners-tail exhaustion. v5 deduplicated by setup signature and confirmed pure-ICT 211/58.3%/+6.96% headline. **Each version's cohort scope was explicitly validated against D.9.3 cohort-translation discipline before drawing conclusions** — saved S29's 5-day Phase 0b investment from compounding error onto wrong cohort.

3. **8-dimension gate audit (`s30_gate_audit_and_ob_attachment.py`).** Per-bucket WR + mean + median + N across gamma_regime, breadth_regime, vix_regime, ict_mtf_context, dte_bucket, expiry_type, time_bucket, symbol. Three gates inverted on live cohort: (a) gamma_regime LONG_GAMMA WR 55.1% N=158 (gated BLOCK) vs SHORT_GAMMA WR 73.3% N=15 (gated PASS) — gating direction correct but rejected bucket is huge; (b) breadth_regime BEARISH-ALIGNED WR 64.7% (gate suppresses); (c) vix_regime HIGH WR 61.2% N=49 (gate suppresses on elevated path). Reasons JSONB cataloged 158× LONG_GAMMA rejection, 37× ENH-88 BULL_FVG cluster block, 89× DTE gate, 172× confidence threshold; only 2 of 211 (0.9%) passed all gates as BUY_CE/BUY_PE with trade_allowed=True. **MERDIAN gate stack rejects 99.4% of pure-ICT high-edge signals.**

4. **OB attachment broken at signal-builder layer (NOT detection layer).** Audit joined `ict_zones` (status='ACTIVE' AND pattern_type IN ('BULL_OB','BEAR_OB'), 35 zones over 8 weeks) against `signal_snapshots` on (symbol, ts within zone validity window, spot inside [zone_low, zone_high]). BULL_OB: 4,882 zone-touches → only 26 tagged BULL_OB (0.5% attachment rate). BEAR_OB: 3,139 zone-touches → **zero** tagged BEAR_OB (0% rate). Most zone-touches tagged NONE or as FVG when adjacent. Detection correct (zones in `ict_zones` have correct pattern_type). Defect at `enrich_signal_with_ict()` or its callers in `build_trade_signal_local.py`. All gate-stack analyses on OB patterns are misleading by construction — the 0.5% sample is non-random. Filed as TD-S30-NEW-3 S1; S31 P0 investigation queued.

5. **Target-days audit `s30_target_days_audit.py` quantified missed P&L on 4 high-leverage days.** May 5/6/13/14 cohort: 89 setups, 89/89 blocked (100%), pooled +544.52pp missed P&L. May 14 SENSEX +400.13pp alone. May 6 14:26-14:50 BULL_OB sequence correctly tagged but action=DO_NOTHING due to ENH-77 NIFTY hard-skip + ENH-77 SENSEX PO3 gate. May 14 11:22+ four-cycle BULL_FVG burst +625% combined, all DO_NOTHING due to ENH-88 standalone block.

**Production patches (5 env-flag toggles deployed Local + AWS via git commit `2604fc2`):**

6. **`apply_s30_patches.py` deployed 5 surgical edits to `build_trade_signal_local.py`.** P1: 4 env-flag module-top reads with default OFF. P2: ENH-76 BEAR_OB MIDDAY PO3_BEARISH gate wrapped `if ENH76_ENABLED and in_midday and ict76 == "BEAR_OB" and action == "BUY_PE":`. P3: ENH-77 BULL_OB AFTERNOON gate wrapped (NIFTY hard-skip + SENSEX PO3_BULLISH). P4: ENH-88 BULL_FVG cluster gate wrapped. P5: post-`enrich_signal_with_ict` override `if TIER_MULT_DISABLE: out["ict_size_mult"]=1.0` + `out["raw"]["tier_mult_disabled"]=True`. AST-validated; 50,620 → 52,127 bytes; commit `2604fc2` 35 lines diff (+30 / -5). Backup `build_trade_signal_local_PRE_S30.py` preserved.

7. **`.env` updated Local + AWS with 4 new flag lines.** `MERDIAN_ENH76_ENABLED=0`, `MERDIAN_ENH77_ENABLED=0`, `MERDIAN_ENH88_ENABLED=0`, `MERDIAN_TIER_MULT_DISABLE=1` (only flag ON). Pre-existing `MERDIAN_SIGNAL_V4=1` + `MERDIAN_ENH55_ENABLED=0` unchanged. AWS-side `.env` reconciliation manual post-`git pull` (gitignored); grep-guarded `cat >>` heredoc pattern applied: `grep -q "MERDIAN_ENH76_ENABLED" .env || cat >> .env <<'ENV_EOF' ... ENV_EOF`.

8. **AWS deployment hit two snags before git pull, codified as operational finding.** (a) SCP from Local Windows blocked by AWS SG IP-whitelist (operator multi-WAN home network with Airtel/BBNL failover). (b) Heredoc paste from Windows clipboard (`Get-Content build_trade_signal_local_PATCHED.py -Raw | Set-Clipboard`) cascaded ~200 bash syntax errors on AWS SSM Session Manager — line-ending mismatch between CRLF clipboard content and bash heredoc parser. **Canonical resolution: git commit Local → push origin/main → AWS git fetch + git pull origin main.** Byte-identical 52,127 bytes both sides; AST OK; grep count 15. Codified as S30 operational finding: AWS sync via git pull is canonical deployment vector; SCP / heredoc paste are last-resort fallbacks with known truncation hazards.

**Documentation (Turn 1 of 3 complete, Turn 2 in flight):**

9. **ADR-009 §S30 case study added** — cohort-translation save (D.9.3 caught its own scope error; S29 Phase 0b 5-day investment on hist_pattern_signals cohort verdict FAIL stands but did NOT transfer to live cohort which is median-positive); new sub-rule "cohort-prior gate hazard" added to §Phase 1 (any gate whose go/no-go decision was derived from a cohort other than the live runtime cohort requires re-validation; env-flag default OFF until N≥30 per-pattern live-cohort validation threshold; cross-link D.8.2 graduated split + D.9.3 cohort-translation as three failure modes).

10. **MERDIAN_Assumption_Register.md §D.13 added** with 5 rows codifying findings: D.13.1 (cohort-translation general principle; ENH-76/77/88 + tier mult env-flag disabled commit `2604fc2`); D.13.2 (persistence inversely correlated with edge — T+10-20m flip best, T+30m worst); D.13.3 (pure-ICT live cohort beats Compendium settled FVG values with statistical significance); D.13.4 (gate stack inverts on gamma/breadth/vix — investigation queued S31+); D.13.5 (OB attachment broken at signal-builder layer; TD-S30-NEW-3 filed). 5 open follow-ups + cross-references to ADR-009 §Phase 1 + §D.9.3 + §D.10.1 + §D.12.2 + TDs. Footer "Last updated" Session 29 → Session 30.

11. **CLAUDE.md v1.20 → v1.21** — new §"Session 30 engineering discoveries" inserted before footer with B29 (cohort-prior gate hazard anti-pattern) + 6 S30 operational findings (cohort-translation §D.9.3 caught itself, OB attachment broken at signal-builder, MERDIAN gate stack inverts edge direction on three context dimensions, patch script + env-flag pattern is canonical "ship reversible disablement" workflow, AWS sync via git pull is canonical deployment vector, `.env` is gitignored requires manual AWS reconciliation). 4 settled-decisions added to footer.

12. **Turn 2 (this rewrite) produces CURRENT.md + session_log.md.** Turn 3 (next operator request) produces tech_debt.md (5 new TDs filed at top of Active section) + MERDIAN_Enhancement_Register.md (ENH-97 RE-EVALUATE queue annotation + ENH candidates for OB attachment fix + replay ENH-88 parity TD ref) + merdian_reference.json (v21 → v22 + S30 change_log + structured session_log entries prepended).

### CRITICAL LESSONS Session 30

- **D.9.3 cohort-translation discipline is a general principle, not specific to ENH-55.** S26 filed it after Exp 20 / ENH-55 hypothesis falsification on live cohort; the codified scope was narrow ("ENH-55 specifically"). S30 demonstrates the principle generalizes: any gate whose empirical justification was derived from a non-production cohort requires explicit re-validation on the live signal-snapshots cohort before deployment. ENH-76/77/88 + tier mult were all promoted on `hist_pattern_signals` 5m-batch cohort evidence and shipped without live-cohort re-validation; D.13.1 + ADR-009 §Phase 1 S30 sub-rule codify the principle as B29 anti-pattern.

- **Cohort-translation check belongs BEFORE deployment decision, not after.** S29 invested 5 days running Phase 0b RR-regime test on `hist_pattern_signals` cohort and reached clean FAIL verdict (χ²=1.56 p≈0.30, median P&L negative both buckets). The verdict was correct on that cohort. S30 measurement on live cohort showed median P&L +3.38% (positive) and statistically meaningful WR uplift over Compendium on both FVG sub-cohorts. Both cohorts' verdicts are valid; they are about different cohorts. The cohort-translation check at S29 start would have caught the gap before the 5-day investment compounded; D.9.3 discipline existed but was scoped narrowly.

- **OB attachment broken at signal-builder layer is the highest-leverage S30 finding.** 4,882 BULL_OB zone-touches → 26 attached (0.5%); 3,139 BEAR_OB zone-touches → zero attached (0%). The detection layer (`ict_zones`) is correct. Defect at attachment time means all gate-stack analyses on OB patterns are working on 0.5% non-random sample; the apparent "BULL_OB doesn't replicate Compendium 84%" finding is unreliable until attachment is fixed. S31 P0 investigation queued (TD-S30-NEW-3). Once fixed, BULL_OB and BEAR_OB sub-cohort N grows from 5 + 0 to estimated 30-80 each, enabling per-OB-pattern re-validation.

- **AWS sync via `git pull` is the canonical deployment vector.** SSH/SCP blocked by IP-whitelist (multi-WAN home network ISP failover). Heredoc paste from Windows clipboard cascades line-ending parse errors in bash SSM Session Manager. The 30-second extra round-trip of git commit Local → push → AWS pull is worth the integrity guarantee — byte-identical state cross-environment, AST validation, grep token-count match. Codified as S30 operational finding.

- **Patch script + env-flag pattern is canonical "ship reversible disablement".** Mirror of S26 ENH-55 pattern. Patch script (`apply_s30_patches.py`) deploys 4 env-flag reads + 4 use-site gates. `.env` documents explicit `=0` lines (auditable vs absence-of-line ambiguous). Re-enable any gate is `.env` edit + restart — no code change required. Reversibility cheaper than code removal. Code paths that fail empirically are still valuable as documentation of what was tried.

- **TD-S30-CANDIDATE-1 was NOT investigated this session.** S29 carry-forward P0_PRIMARY was "live `compute_gamma_metrics_local.py` Cr unit regression investigation." S30 pivoted to live cohort question first based on operator concern. TD-S30-CANDIDATE-1 remains open as S31 P0_PRIMARY carry-forward (not retracted, not investigated — un-actioned). Codified honestly here to prevent next-session drift.

- **MERDIAN_TIER_MULT_DISABLE=1 default** — same rationale; tier multiplier forces `ict_size_mult=1.0` overriding `enrich_signal_with_ict()`; do not revert to tier-conditional sizing without live-cohort per-tier WR distribution evidence.

### What Session 29 did, in 17 bullets

**Firefighting 2026-05-14 (compound incident + concurrent Dhan storm + concurrent spot gap):**

1. **TD-NEW-A RESOLVED** (in-flight, S1) — `market_ticks` retention runaway → 62 GB bloat → INSERT timeouts cascading into 6+ hour breadth outage. Pg_cron `delete-old-market-ticks` jobid 45 had been failing every weekday since at least 2026-04-30 with `statement_timeout` (Postgres 57014). 14+ consecutive failures accumulated `market_ticks` to 62 GB (22 heap + 40 indexes). At that size, `ws_feed_zerodha.py` bulk INSERT also began exceeding statement_timeout, producing the cascade. Fix: `pkill -9 -f ws_feed_zerodha.py` + `TRUNCATE public.market_ticks` (62 GB → 856 kB in <1s — DDL primitive; DELETE itself would have timed out at this size) + `cron.unschedule(45)` + `cron.schedule('prune-market-ticks', '*/30 * * * 1-5', $$DELETE FROM public.market_ticks WHERE ts < now() - interval '1 hour'$$)` → jobid 46 (cadence 1/day → 1/30min, horizon 2days → 1hour decouples worst-case DELETE workload from cron cadence). Codified as CLAUDE.md B25 (TRUNCATE vs DELETE) + Topology §6.10 + §6.11 + OI-12 RE-RESOLVED block.

2. **Token-in-memory Root Cause A surfaced**. Long-running `ws_feed_zerodha.py` held prior day's token loaded from 09:14 IST cron until manually killed at 18:09 IST. Operator pattern-matched first to 2026-04-22 incident (skipped Step 2 of token refresh) and re-ran token-refresh sequence twice with no improvement; `kite.profile()` returned AUTH OK both times. Codified as CLAUDE.md B24 (`.env` edits don't propagate to running processes) + Topology §6.10 new gotcha + TD-NEW-F closure via 5 verbatim markdown edits to `runbook_update_kite_flow.md`.

3. **Compound-incident pattern-match trap surfaced** (codified as S29 operational finding). Third diagnostic step (log tail of restarted feeder after `pkill -9 -f`) revealed the independent second root cause via `Supabase write error 500: {code:57014,message:canceling statement due to statement timeout}` — distinct from the token-in-memory symptom. The 2-attempt-no-change rule generalizes B17's 3-refutation rule to compound incidents: if a hypothesis-matched fix produces no behavioral change in 2 consecutive attempts, the hypothesis is likely incomplete or the incident is compound.

4. **Concurrent Dhan 429 storm — TD-080 PROMOTED to S1 RECURRING**. 99/808 `ingest_option_chain_local.py` cycles failed with `status=429 path=/v2/optionchain response={data:{805:Too many requests. Further requests may result in the user being blocked.},status:failed}` between 11:06-15:25 IST (4h19m duration, 12.3% failure rate). Same token same endpoint same alternating-window symptom shape as S22 2026-05-07 (151/299) + S28 2026-05-13 (alluded); per-token rate-limit instability hypothesis corroborated across 3 sessions. ENH spec for rate-limit-aware retry layer + circuit breaker (exponential backoff + per-token quota tracking + 429-pause circuit breaker) is P0 carry-forward to S30.

5. **Concurrent spot bar gap backfill (17 rows)**. Daily audit at 16:00 IST returned `OVERALL: FAIL` on 4 thresholds + WARN on 492 crashes across 6 scripts. Attribution: 77% breadth cascade Incident 1; 20% Dhan 429 storm; 1.4% TD-NEW-H NULL `expiry_date`; 0.6% TD-NEW-J/TD-083 OUTSIDE_MARKET_HOURS; ~1% misc. **False-positive scare during diagnosis (codified as B27)**: initial gap-detection SQL used `SELECT generate_series(timezone('Asia/Kolkata','2026-05-14 09:15:00'), ..., interval '1 minute')` which actually generates 14:45 IST → 20:59 IST (5h30m forward-shifted because string parsed as UTC by default; `timezone()` converts UTC value to IST display but underlying timestamptz unchanged); query produced 245 phantom missing minutes. Codified: build expected-time series in UTC at actual UTC times and let join handle TZ conversion in output formatting only; never use `timezone()` cast to construct IST series from wall-clock string. Real 17 gaps after corrected query: 10:21-10:24 + 10:27 + 10:42-10:44 + SENSEX 15:29; backfill via MALPHA-side `backfill_spot_zerodha.py` after Python heredoc file repair (earlier sed had corrupted multi-line `BACKFILL_DATES = [...]` list literal); 750-row idempotent upsert; net 17 new in `market_spot_snapshots`.

6. **TD-061 + TD-063 RESOLVED** (after S17/S18 partial closure was insufficient — body-state-vs-footer-claim divergence codified as Doc Protocol v4 Rule N candidate). S18 footer claimed TD-061 RESOLVED; body remained Active. S23 audit confirmed only 4/15 migrated; S29 audit found 19 tasks with only 4/19 on pythonw at S29-start. `migrate_to_pythonw.ps1` v2 (v1 abandoned due to regex shell-redirection capture bug — greedy regex captured `>>`, `2>&1`, etc. as pythonw args; v2 whitelisted argument shapes + blacklisted shell metas; codified as B28). Phase 1: 13 .bat-wrapping tasks via regex-extract. Phase 2: 4 wrapper layers dropped, re-pointed at `pythonw.exe` direct invocation. New `run_ict_htf_zones_daily.py` Python orchestrator replaces `.bat` for ICT_HTF_Zones_0845. Settings tightened on 18/19 tasks. State at close: 13/19 actions on pythonw; 18/19 settings tightened; 5 residual flashes are low-frequency sources documented as known limitations.

**Production code patches:**

7. **TD-NEW-I RESOLVED** — `merdian_daily_audit.py` thresholds `spot_bars_per_symbol_min: 370 → 365` + `market_spot_snapshots_per_symbol: 370 → 365` via `patch_s29_td_new_i_j_v2.py`. Audit was flagging FAIL on ~98% coverage days (367/375 NIFTY + 366/375 SENSEX). Operational reality: 375 bars/day theoretical max but typical day has 2-5 known gap minutes from operational timing windows.

Patch v1 abandoned due to regex undercatch + docstring breakage risk; v2 applied via `patch_s29_td_new_i_j_v2.py`. AST-validated.

**Build work 2026-05-14 → 2026-05-16:**

Stage 1 `backfill_volatility_snapshots.py` wrote 19,520 rows full year Apr 2025 → Mar 2026 (inverse-BS IV solve from `hist_atm_option_bars_5m` + `hist_spot_bars_5m`; bridges 5h30m IST-as-UTC vs real UTC offset between hist tables and live writer). Stage 2 `backfill_vol_analytics.py` wrote 24,758 rows. Regime distribution LOW 38.1% / COMPRESSED 32.7% / FAIR 15.1% / HIGH 14.1%.

10. **Phase 0b verdict on ADR-002 v2 P7 4-way regime gate = FAIL**. `phase0b_rr_conditional_wr.py` joined 1,968 regime-tagged signals from `hist_pattern_signals × vol_analytics × hist_atm_option_bars_5m`. Overall WR 46.2%. χ²=1.56 p≈0.30 across LOW/COMPRESSED/FAIR/HIGH regimes. **FAIL** — RR-conditional WR is not statistically distinguishable from baseline.

11. **Phase 0b salvage test on COMPRESSED veto binary = FAIL on power**. `phase0b_compressed_veto.py` direction right but variance dominates; bootstrap CI [-3.36, +17.69]pp **INCLUDES ZERO**; median P&L negative both buckets. **Verdict: definitive FAIL.** ICT cohort itself is median-negative across all regimes (buyer-edge lives in tails not at median).

12. **ENH-97 pivoted from signal-time gating to logging-only** (status update PROPOSED → SHIPPED-AS-LOGGING). `vol_analytics` regime column written for future analysis; no signal-time gate. Codified principle: definitive FAIL verdict on a Phase 0b dimension means abandoning that dimension as a gate, not retrying with different parameters — variance dominates the signal at this cohort size, more parameter tweaks ≠ statistical power.

13. **Critical data-source finding + TD-094 RECLASSIFIED-STALE**. Operator firmly corrected confusion during gamma backfill design: `option_chain_snapshots` + `market_spot_snapshots` are live-only capture tables (Feb 2026+); vendor-backfilled 14-month historical data lives in `hist_option_bars_1m` + `hist_spot_bars_1m`. OI verification query confirmed 99.9% populated across all 12 months (avg ~1M, max 66M). Vendor data replaced broken S22 Kite backfill (when exactly is unknown — no commit marker in scope). **Unblocks** Phase 0b gamma-context dimensions P1 LONG_GAMMA + P3 flip_distance + P5 PINNED + ENH-80 per-strike GEX. Codified S29 operational finding: when a TD claims a data limitation, verify against current table state before designing around the limitation.

Reimplements live writer math standalone with TD-NEW-2 Parts A+B (Part A sanity guard + Part B walk-from-ATM) + TD-NEW-3 (`/1e7` Cr conversion) explicit citations to commit `241f943`. Unblocked by new DB index `ix_hist_option_bars_1m_bar_ts_strike ON hist_option_bars_1m (bar_ts, strike, option_type)` created 2026-05-15 via direct DB connection with `SET statement_timeout=0` (PostgREST 8s timeout doesn't apply); 54.8M-row table required custom index for per-cycle indexed lookups.

Ratio matches exactly the `/1e7` Cr conversion that TD-NEW-3 was supposed to apply. **Live writer apparently regressed at some point between S27 close and S29 start.** Filed as S30 P0_PRIMARY investigation: `git log -p compute_gamma_metrics_local.py` between `241f943` and present HEAD; identify regression commit; restore `/1e7` line; smoke test.

17. **CLAUDE.md v1.19 → v1.20** — B24 (`.env` edits do not propagate to running consumer processes) + B25 (TRUNCATE vs DELETE on bloated tables — DELETE itself times out at scale, TRUNCATE is O(1) DDL primitive) + B26 (pg_cron failures invisible by default — `cron.job_run_details` needs polling daemon or session-start gate) + B27 (timezone-series with `timezone()` cast of wall-clock IST strings produces phantom misses — construct UTC series at actual UTC times instead) + B28 (regex capture of arbitrary trailing tokens unsafe in command-injection contexts — whitelist argument shapes + blacklist shell metacharacters). 10 S29 operational findings appended. 11 settled-decisions footer entries. **14-file doc-close pack** per Doc Protocol v4 Rule 3 + Rule 9 (full file-size audit disk-vs-new shown for each; no-crunch / no-append discipline maintained throughout).

### CRITICAL LESSONS Session 29

1. **Compound incidents pattern-match trap.** When operator pattern-matched first hypothesis (token-stale from 2026-04-22) and tried fix twice with no improvement, the third diagnostic step (log tail of restarted process) revealed the independent second root cause. **2-attempt-no-change rule** (generalizes B17 3-refutation rule to compound incidents): if a hypothesis-matched fix produces no behavioral change in 2 consecutive attempts, the hypothesis is likely incomplete or the incident is compound. Codified as S29 operational finding.

2. **TD body-state must match footer-claim (Doc Protocol v4 candidate Rule N).** S18 footer claimed TD-061 RESOLVED; body remained Active section; S23 audit confirmed only 4/15 migrated; S29 audit found 19 tasks and only 4/19 on pythonw at S29-start. Filing rule for any future TD resolution: body block must be moved to Resolved section AND closure block must contain patch script / commit / verification evidence. Footer-only resolutions are not allowed and must be re-opened in the next session.

3. **TRUNCATE vs DELETE is a structural primitive distinction.** For tables under statement_timeout pressure, DELETE itself times out at scale (>10 GB on Supabase with default statement_timeout). TRUNCATE is O(1) DDL primitive — 62 GB → 856 kB in <1s. Codified as CLAUDE.md B25. Operational rule: when a maintenance DELETE has been failing repeatedly with statement_timeout, the recovery is TRUNCATE not "increase the timeout" — by the time symptoms surface, the DELETE workload is already too large.

4. **pg_cron failures invisible by default (B26).** `cron.job_run_details` is not polled by any MERDIAN telemetry layer. `merdian_pipeline_alert_daemon.py` doesn't query the `cron` schema. Telegram alert daemon doesn't subscribe to cron-failure events. Without alerting, the next pg_cron failure class will also escalate silently before operator-visible symptoms surface. **Mandatory session-start checklist SQL** (added to Topology §6.11): `SELECT jobname, status, return_message, start_time FROM cron.job_run_details d JOIN cron.job j USING (jobid) WHERE start_time > now() - interval '7 days' AND status != 'succeeded' ORDER BY start_time DESC` — empty result = healthy; any rows = investigate. TD-NEW-B (S1) implementation queued as P1 S30.

5. **B27 timezone-series with `timezone()` cast of wall-clock IST strings produces phantom misses.** `timezone('Asia/Kolkata', '2026-05-14 09:15:00')` parses the string as UTC by default, then converts UTC to IST display — but the underlying timestamptz is the original UTC value shifted +5:30, not the intended 09:15 IST = 03:45 UTC. **Operational rule:** build expected-time series in UTC at actual UTC times (e.g. `'2026-05-14 03:45:00+00'::timestamptz` for 09:15 IST trading-start) and let join handle TZ conversion in output formatting only. Never use `timezone()` cast to construct IST series from wall-clock string literal.

6. **B28 regex capture of arbitrary trailing tokens unsafe in command-injection contexts.** `migrate_to_pythonw.ps1` v1 used greedy regex `(?<rest>(\s+\S+)*)\s*$` to capture pythonw args after the script path — captured `>>`, `2>&1`, etc. as pythonw args. Would have caused silent crashes on first scheduled fire. v2 fix: whitelist argument shapes (must start with `-` or be a `.py` file path) + blacklist shell metacharacters. **Operational rule:** when generating command lines from parsed templates, never trust greedy "rest of line" captures; always validate argument shapes against an allowlist.

7. **Source-of-truth pivot: live capture tables vs hist tables.** `option_chain_snapshots` + `market_spot_snapshots` are live-only (Feb 2026+); vendor-backfilled historical data lives in `hist_option_bars_1m` + `hist_spot_bars_1m`. Confusing the two during gamma backfill design produced wrong "data is sparse" conclusion initially; operator firmly corrected. **Operational rule:** when a TD claims a data limitation (e.g., TD-094 "Kite historical_data doesn't return OI"), verify against current table state before designing around the limitation — vendor data refresh may have closed the gap. **Codified to CLAUDE.md S29 operational findings.**

8. **Custom-index requirement for 54.8M-row tables.** `hist_option_bars_1m` per-cycle indexed lookup required `CREATE INDEX ix_hist_option_bars_1m_bar_ts_strike ON hist_option_bars_1m (bar_ts, strike, option_type)` — without it, sequential scans exceeded statement_timeout. Created via direct DB connection with `SET statement_timeout=0` (PostgREST 8s timeout doesn't apply to direct sessions). **Operational rule:** schema changes that exceed default statement_timeout require direct DB connection bypassing PostgREST; document the bypass in Topology.

9. **Phase 0b FAIL means abandon the dimension, not retry with different parameters.** ICT cohort itself is median-negative across all regimes (buyer-edge lives in tails not at median). Variance dominates the signal at this cohort size; more parameter tweaks ≠ statistical power. ENH-97 pivoted from signal-time gating to logging-only as the principled response to a definitive FAIL verdict. **Operational rule:** when Phase 0b returns FAIL with bootstrap CI including zero, the dimension is dead as a gate; ship as logging if data has future value, otherwise drop entirely. Codified as candidate for ADR-009 calibration discipline content.
